 Hence i chose the character of Parvati Bai
 is kairactor main kai aayam hai
 'she says that very little has been written about Parvati Bai in history
 parvati bai kairactor ko ashutosh goarikar ne gadha he
 According to this, they are my history book
 wo is film ke director hai
 Kriti, 'parvati Bai was a Brahmin and married the Maratha warrior Sadashiv Rao
 shaadi ke baad parvati bai ne rajgaraane kaa jivan apanaaya tha
 Parvati Bai was a feminist woman at that time and she spoke of equality between man and woman
 ' kriti kaa maananaa he ki unke liye parvati bai kaa kairactor karnaa aasaan isliye ho gaya tha ki hamadonon ke vichaaron main kaaphi mail he
 This made it easy for him to put every look on screen
 lekin parvati bai or mujhamen ek antar yah he ki unki tarah main khulkar pyaar kaa izhaar nahin kar sakati
 Kriti, who has done light, laughable and social films till now, has learned to speak Marathi from Ketki for Parvati Bai
 unka maananaa he ki har mahila ek hi tarah kii hoti hai
 But because of the language, their body language changes
 yahi vajah he ki marathi bhashaa par zyada jor diya
 Kriti, 'ashutosh Gowariker is the master of period films
 unhone jodha akbar banaai jo shreshth film he
 The characters of his period film are contemporary
 khaskar mahila kairactor par wo bahut mehnat karte hai or unhen kaaphi majboot paksh ke taur par pesh bhi karte hai
 After Jodha, the character of Parvati Bai will also affect everyone
 ' ashutosh director se pehle actor bhi rahe hai to aise main unke saath kaam karne main kitni sahuuliyat hui? is par kriti apana anubhav saajha karte hue kahati hai ki ashutosh imoshan ko actor kii tarah hi baahar laate hai
 He is a wonderful director
 kool rahete hai or kabhi bhi actor ke saamne sakaaratmak hi rahete hai
 This makes the actor always comfortable
 ek or baat yah ki jab unhone mujhe parvati bai ke rup main chunaa to mujhe laga ki aakhir kyon mujhe is kairactor ke liye sin kiya
 During the shooting it became clear how strong his connoisseur eyes are
 is film main sadashiv raav kii bhoomika main arjuna kapur hai to gopika bai ke role main padmini kolhapure ke saath unka saas-bahu vaala rishta he
 Kriti was nervous in front of senior actor Zeenat Aman who plays Sakina Begum
 lekin shooting ke dauraan jinat ne unhen kaaphi sahaj rakhaa
 There has also been controversy over a spoken dialogue of Kriti regarding Mastani in the film
 is par kriti safai detii hai ki trailor main yah seen or samvaad puure nahin hai
 People are misunderstood by this
 puri film dekhne ke baad yah galatfahami mit jaaegi
 With this film of Kriti, another film Husband Wife and She is also releasing in which she is in guest appearance
 is vajah se wo is film ke bare main baat karne se bachati hai
 Kriti has a great appetite for acting and she wants to do all kinds of characters
 unako abhi kisi byopic ke liye ofer nahin mila he
 But she wants to live Madhubala, Meena Kumari and Indira Gandhi because her life story is different from any woman
 kriti apni aane vaali ek film mimi kaa zikr karne se nahin chookti hai
 She says that this film is close to her heart and she would like to do more such films
 *** Once again a tragic incident has come out from Darbhanga in Bihar on Saturday when the 5 children who went to bathe in the river started drowning slowly and all five of them disappeared in sight and then these five died
 marane vaale sabhi bacchon kii umr 10 se 12 saal ke bich bataai ja rahi he
 This incident is from Madhopur village of Kamtaul police station of Darbhanga
 yaha se praapt jaankaree ke anusaar is gaanv ke paanchon bachche nadi main nahaane ke liye gaye the
 According to eyewitnesses, when one of the five children started drowning, in order to save them, the other children also jumped into the river and all drowned and died on sight
 is ghatana ke turant baad gaanv waalon ne police ko is baat kii jaankaree di or phir police mauka-e-vaardaat par pahunchakar paanchon bacchon ke shavon ko pani se nikaala
 Police suspect that in addition to these five children, more children may have gone missing due to drowning in the water, so the help of swimmers is being taken to search for them
 gauratlab he ki pichley hafte hi darbhanga ke ghanashyampur or kusheshwarasthaan thana kshetra main alag-alag ghatnaon main saat ladakiyon kii doobane kii khabar saamne ai he
 Including the incident of last week and today, so far 12 children have died due to drowning in the river of Darbhanga
 jharkhand ke mukhyamantri raghuvar das guhaar lagane pahunche vyakti par hi gussa ho gaye
 Not only this, he publicly asked a helpless person to be taken out of the program
 darasal is shaks kii beti ne aatmahatya kar lee thi or vah insaaf kii guhaar ke liye raghuvar das se milane pahunchaa tha
 In fact, Jharkhand Chief Minister Raghuvar Das reached the BJP Mahila Morcha program on International Women's Day
 is dauraan vahaan suicide karne vaali ek ladki ke pita pahunche
 On seeing the Chief Minister, that person started crying
 haalanki das ne pehle unhen samajhaayaa or insaaf kaa bharosa dilaayaa
 But the Chief Minister got angry after repeatedly pleading
 iske baad raghuvar das ne peedit pita ko buree tarah dutkaarte hue us par raajnneeti karne kaa aarope lagaaya
 Also asked to remove that person from the program
 ye he maamladansal beete guuruuvaar ranchi main koching institute ke hostel main chaatra kii sandigdh haalat main maut ho gai thi
 However, the postmortem report has revealed suicide
 jabaki police kii jaanch main saamne aayaa ki maut se thik pehle vah ek ladke se baat kar rahi thi
 Police has registered an FIR against four people in this case
 saath hi peedita ke bwoyfriend se bhi poochtacha kii
 This is the father's accusation of the father that his daughter has been murdered and the police have met the criminals
 is baat par mukhyamantri bhadak gaye or ulataa peedit ko hi daant laga di
 a stampede occurred in Aurangabad, Bihar during Chhath Puja
 is dauraan 2 bacchon kii maut ho gai he
 Apart from this, some people are also injured in the incident
 yah haadasa dev prakhand mukhyalay sthit suryakund ke paas kaa he
 Police are trying to investigate the cause of the stampede
 is bich jile ke dm rahul ranjan mahivaal or espi deepak baranwaal ne mritkon ke parijanon se milakar unhen dhankos bandhaaya or is ghatana ko afsosjanak qaraar diya
 According to officials, this chaos occurred due to overcrowding
 unhone kaha ki mritkon ke parijanon ko niyamanukul muaavje kaa tatkaal bhugtan kiya jayega or aage aisi ghatana kii punrariti na ho isaki puri vyavastha kii jaaegi
 This is not the first time in Bihar when such a big accident happened on the occasion of Chhath
 isse pehle saal 2012 main bhi chhath puja ke dauraan patna main ek haadasa hua tha
 Where the bridge made of bamboo bats was broken
 bhagdad machane se 18 logon kii maut ho gai thi
 The deceased children have been identified in the accident
 mritkon main patna ke bihata kaa ek 6 varshiya balak or doosraa bhojpur ke sahaar kii ek dedh saal kii bacchee shaamil he
 After this incident, the Bihar administration has once again come under the scanner
 eespi keshav chandra goswami dwaara shikaayat darj karaane kii guhaar lekar gai dushkarm peedit mahila kaa apmaan karne ke maamle par khed jataate hue eespi se spashtikaaran maanga he
 Uttar Pradesh Additional Director General of Police (law and Order) Ram Kumar Vishwakarma told reporters that asp's remarks cannot be justified at all
 ham police vibhaag kii taraf se iske liye maafee maangate hai
 He said that the Director General of Police ASP Goswami has ordered clarification within two days
 uske baad aage kii karrwai hogi
 Vishwakarma said that the investigation of the incident has been started by registering a case against the accused of rape on the complaint of the victim woman
 gauratlab he ki devaria jile ke banakata thana kshetra ke dalanchhapra gaanv main adhed mahila ke saath do din pehle ek vyakti ne kathith rup se dushkarm karne ke baad jaan se maarane kii koshish kii
 The woman, who arrived at the Bankata police station with a complaint, pleaded to register a case with ASP Goswami on Thursday evening after not hearing

 mantralay ne kuch associationon ko di gai inakam tex main chhot ab waapas le lee he

 guuruuvaar ko jari ek elaan ke tahat saurashtra cricket association, baroda cricket association, kerala cricket association or maharashtra cricket association ko tex main di gai chhot waapas le lee gai he
 According to the information, the income tax authorities have taken this decision after carefully watching the work of all
 adhikari is nishkarsh par pahunche hai ki ye association jis tarah kii gatividhiyaan chalaa rahe hai vah darasal camershal yani maudrik laabh ke liye kiye jane vaale kaam hai
 In such a situation, they can no longer get the same facilities after the change in section 2 (15) of the Income Tax Act, 1961
 iske saath hi unke pichley maamalon kii bhi jaanch hogi taaki yah pataa chal sake ki unhone tex main chhot sahi aadhaar par liya tha yaa nahin

 Know these special things about the first satellite 'aryabhata'
 
 - The first satellite of the country, Aryabhata, was named after Indira Gandhi after the great astronomer and mathematician Aryabhatta
 - 17 saal baad 11 farvari 1992 main isane dobaaraa prithvi ke vaataavaran main pravesh kiya
 ISRO is trying to reconnect with GSAT-6A ISRO - Aryabhata weighing 360 kg was sent to space with the help of Inter Cosmos rocket of Soviet Union
 - is upgrah ko lekar sabase ascharyajanak baat yah he ki upgrah ke liye ek shauchalay kaa kayakalp kiya gaya or vahaan iskaa kaam chalaa

 It was through this satellite that ISRO gained experience of operating in space

 After this, the first election was held here in 2009
 pehle chunaav se hi yahaan congress, bijepi or maharashtra nav nirmaan sena ke bich trikoniya muqabla hota rahaa he
 If you look at the figures, in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, Kapil Patil of BJP won the election here
 unhen 4,11,070 vot hasil hue the
 He defeated Vishwanath Patil of Congress
 unhen 3,01,620 vot hasil hue the
 At the same time, Suresh Mahatre of MNS finished third
 unhen 93,647 vot mili the
 Let us tell that due to a triangular contest in Bhiwandi seat, no single party can win unilaterally
 pichley kuch chunaav se yahaan congress or bijepi kaa khel manase bigaadti rahi he
 a similar equation was confused in the 2009 Lok Sabha elections
 yahaan congress ke suresh taavare chunaav jite the
 He received 1,82,789 votes
 taavare ne bijepi ke jagannatha patil ko chunaav haraaya
 Patil received 1,41,425 votes
 vahiin, tisare sthaan par rahe devraj maharaatre unhen 1,07,090 vot mili the
 How to change Bhiwandi's equation
 
 
 
 Bhiwandi seat in Thane district was a part of Dahanu Lok Sabha constituency before delimitation
 dahanu se alag hone ke baad bhiwandi main wo teen vidhansabha ai jahaan bijepi kaa dabadabaa rahaa
 This is the reason why BJP has kept this seat with them after alliance with Shiv Sena
 maaloom ho ki 1999 main bijepi ke chintaman vanagaa ne dahanu loksabhaa seat par congress ke di em shingda ko haraaya
 Since then, bjp's dominance in Dahanu has increased
 lekin parisemen ke baad jin ilaakon main bijepi kaa dabadabaa tha unamem se teen vidhansabha seat jawahar, dahanu or igatpuri bhiwandi loksabhaa se cat gai
 The effect of which also appeared in the 2009 Lok Sabha elections in Bhiwandi
 yahaan bijepi kii haar hui congress ke suresh taavare jite
 While Jagannath Patil of BJP had to face defeat
 kya he vidhansabha siton kii sthiti
 
 
 The Congress and NCP have always dominated the 6 assembly seats of Bhiwandi Lok Sabha seat
 lekin pichley kuch chunaav se yahaan shivasena or bijepi ne dam bharaa he
 The equations have changed here in the last assembly election
 bhiwandi gramin or bhiwandi east vidhansabha par shivasena kaa raaj he
 So Bhiwandi West, Kalyan West and Murbad are ruled by BJP
 jabaki ensipi yahaan kii shahpur seat par kabiz he
 Researchers have discovered that Akkermensia muciniphila, a species of bacterium present in the human intestine, provides greater protection against various cardiovascular risk factors by using it as pasteurization
 patrika 'nechar medicine' main prakashit is nishkarsh ke mutabik, lauven uniwarsity kii research team ne maanav sharir main prabhavi bacteria par adhyayan kiya
 42 participants were nominated for this and 32 completed this test
 shodhakartaaon ne mote pratibhaagiyon ko akkarmensia diya, in sabhi main diabetes tip 2 or metabolic syndrome dekhe gaye
 That is, there were risk factors related to heart diseases
 pratibhaagiyon ko teen samoohon main baant diya gaya- ek jinhone jivit bacteria liya or do jinhone paschurikrut bacteria liya- in donon samoohon ke sadasyon main apane khan-paan or shaareerik gatividhiyon main parivartan karne ke liye kaha gaya
 They were given as Akkermansia nutritional supplements
 akkarmensia kaa seven in pratibhaagiyon ko teen maheene tak lagaataar karnaa tha
 Researchers found that this supplement was easy to eat and no side effects were observed in living and pasteurized bacteria-consuming groups
 paschurikrut bacteria ne pratibhaagiyon main diabetes 2 or dil kii bimariyon ke khatre ko kaaphi had tak kam kar diya
 This also showed improvement in liver health, also a decline in the body weight of the participants (usually 2
 3 kilo) dekhi gai or inke saath hi saath cholesterol ke str main bhi kami ai

 agar maaya sarkaar ne pathar or murtiyon par paisa bahaane ke bajaay rojgaar srijan par dhyaan diya hota to aaj lakhon yuvakon ko rojgaar mil gaya hota or hamaari sarkaar ko aaj berogari bhatta nahin baantnaa padataa
 Akhilesh said that the BSP government pushed Uttar Pradesh back

 sapa ke pradesh pravaktaa rajendra choudhary ne kaha ki ye mayawati ke apane sanskaar hai jinamein chaar baar mukhyamantri ke pad par rahane ke baad bhi badlaav nahin aayaa he
 Chaudhary said that the organizers of today's rally of BSP were the same former ministers who are caught in corruption investigations and are scared of going to jail
 apane gunahon par pardaa daalane or aam janata ko gumraah karne ke liye hi yah nautanki hui he
